3_skip
Pretty much FISTrio visit mom and Serena in Serenaverse. Dracula is woken up and cursed Maria, Shirabe and Serena to turn them into his loyal monster. Kirika's Phonic Gain wakes up Kresnik, the spirit of the man who beat dracula and who is bound in the silver bullet relic that kept Dracula sealed (when the thing was pulled out Dracula was free to wake up). Kirika has to kill Dracula or the FISGirls cant be saved. She gets help from ChrisBikki. Originally Krsnik granted/transferred them knowledge/skills but Kirika merges the Silver Bullet directly into Igalima, gets her duorelic and kills Dracula saving the day. The story is translated/posted on YT so you can look it up <:KirikaDess:336656774251806720>
Yeah pretty much is the Gears combining a relic with their respective symphogear to make a DuoRelic Mode
Hibiki - Gungnir-Mjolnir
Basa - AnH-Murakumo (aka Kusanagi. Same/similar sword Fudo used)
Chris - Ichiaval-Nehushtan Staff (do not confuse with the Nehushtan Armor from S1 though their similar)
Maria - Airgetlam-Hermes Sword
Shirabe -Shulshagana-Yasakani no Magatama
Kirika - Igalima- Silver Bullet (used to kill/seal dracula)
Kanade - Gungnir-Brinsingamen
Miku - Aegis Shield
Serena - Airgetlam-Gleipnir
Obviously XDU taking some liberties with some/most of the relic myths. Most relics are from Alternate Worlds they visit

The temple of B√™l, the Babylonian Zeus [...] was still in existence in my time. It has a solid central tower, one stadium square, with a second erected on top of it and then a third, and so on up to eight. All eight towers can be climbed by a spiral way running round the outside, and about half way up there are seats for those who make the ascent to rest on. On the summit of the topmost tower stands a great temple with a fine large couch in it, richly covered, and a golden table beside it. The shrine contains no image, and no one spends the night there except (if we may believe that Chaldaeans who are the priests of B√™l) one Babylonian woman, all alone, whoever it may be that the god has chosen. 'Vanessa' is a name that was adopted to refer to a genus of butterfly.
    Vanessa's last name references the Villa Diodati. It served as inspiration for the 1818 gothic horror Frankenstein written by Mary Shelley, who visited the villa with friends to tell stories.
'Elsa' is derived from 'Elizabeth', which means roughly 'I have pledged my oath to God'.
    'B√™te' means 'beast' in French. It additionally references the Beast of G√©vaudan (French: La B√™te du G√©vaudan). This beast is a man-eating werewolf that terrorized the former province of G√©vaudan (modern-day d√©partement of Loz√®re and part of Haute-Loire), in the Margeride Mountains in south-central France between 1764 and 1767.
the names not that special i guess but the info on the last names is interesting if true
oh they also have name info for vanessa and elsa
'Millaarc' is an anagram of 'Carmilla', the titular character of an Irish gothic novella published in 1872. Carmilla, previously known as 'Mircalla' or 'Millarca', was a vampire who preyed on and made romantic advances towards the female protagonist, Laura.
    'Cranstoun' seems to reference Countess Purgastall Jane Cranstoun, the fiance of Joseph von Hammer-Purgstall, an Austrian orientalist and historian from Styria, the same as Millaarc's origin. Jane Cranstoun was a possible inspiration for Carmilla. 'Cranstoun' is also similar to 'Karnstein', Carmilla's last name.

One who engages in this fallacy is said to be "attacking a straw man". 
The typical straw man argument creates the illusion of having completely refuted or defeated an opponent's proposition through the covert replacement of it with a different proposition (i.e., "stand up a straw man") and the subsequent refutation of that false argument ("knock down a straw man") instead of the opponent's proposition."

Aaand now you know the full titles and why we simply call them YuYuYu, NoWaYu, WaSuYu and KuMeYu. Its just easier
YuYuYu - Yuuki Yuuna wa Yuusha de Aru (Yuki Yuna is a Hero) - main story with main cast
NoWaYu - Nogi Wakaba wa Yuusha de Aru (Nogi Wakaba is a Hero) - prequel novel of ||the first hero team||
WaSuYu - Washio Sumi wa Yuusha de Aru (Washio Sumi is a Hero) - prequel novel before the events of the main series which was made into the trilogy movie that was split into episodes in the 2nd season
KuMeYu - Kusunoki Mebuki wa Yuusha de Aru (Kusunoki Mebuki is a Hero) - side-story novel taking place inbetween the main events following ||the failures known as weeds||

To clarify a few details -
S2 is divided into Washio Sumi Chapter (Washio no Shou) and Hero Chapter (Yuusha no Shou). Washio is the prequel to S1 and it was originally 3 movies. you can watch either the tv version (6 episodes) or movies (3 movies). Hero Chapter is the sequel to S1 and is 6 episodes. there is an "Ep.0" which is just a recap.

S3 is called Dai-Mankai Chapter (Dai-Mankai no Shou) and is 12 episodes. it acts as extra/expanded content to s2 plus adapts 2 light novel stories. Kusunoki Mebuki which is a side-story taking place between s1-s2 and Nogi Wakaba which is a farther prequel. the ln adaptions are fast-paced and in the case of the Nogi Wakaba its crap (which sucks cause best ln).

Tried to go through the episodes for a refresher and find some kind of mixed watch order for S2-S3.

Easy watch order - S1 > S2 Washio Sumi Chapter.

ok now here is where shit gets a lil complicated

S2 Hero Chapter EP1-2 > S3 Dai-Mankai EP1-4 (i wouldve suggested this first but the halfway point/final of Ep.4 spoilers the end of Hero 2).
Hero Ep.3 > Dai Ep.5-8 > Hero Ep.4-5
Dai Ep.9-12 (you can watch Hero Ep.6 after for a few extra bits of cut dialogue and a different epilogue but Dai 9-12 is overall the better end/final)

English Fire Bomber CD direct from the wiki
ENGLISH FIRE. All the songs on this album have been redone in English by the band Fire Bomber American. Instead of simply being English versions of Fire Bomber songs, the makers of Macross have created an English version of the band Fire Bomber. In the Macross universe, Fire Bomber American is a band on the English-speaking fleet Macross 11 that claims that the Macross 7 Fire Bomber is a rip-off of it. The singers for this band are also different.[14] According to the fictional Macross continuity Lynn Kaifun, a character from the first TV series from 1982 (who was Lynn Minmay's cousin and also her former manager) is the creator and manager of Fire Bomber American.
